MAR SGOM PA'I TSE RTOG BCAS YIN KYANG, GOMS BYA LA GSAL SNANG JE
CHER SONG STE BSKYED RIM PHRA RAGS MTHAR PHYIN PA NA, DKYIL
'KHOR GYI 'KHOR

LO'I SNANG BA YID SHES LA MNGON SUM DU SHAR BA'I RTOG MED DU
'GYUR BA YIN PA'I PHYIR TE, DE'I TSE DE 'DRA BA'I YID SHES DE
RANG GI SNANG BA LA MNGON SUM TSAD MA YIN PA'I PHYIR TE, RIGS
PA'I DBANG PHYUG GIS, YANG DAG MIN

PA'ANG BSGOMS PA YI, ,STONGS KYIS SPRUL PA RTOG MED DANG, ,GSAL
BAR SNANG BA CAN DU MTHONG, ZHES GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR, 'O NA GANG
DANG BRAL BAS PHYAG RGYA CHEN PO'I DNGOS GRUB MI 'THOB PA RDO
RJE'I RNAL 'BYOR DE JI LTA BU ZHE NA

DE'I LAN STON PA LA, DU BA LA SOGS MTSAN MA DAG DANG NI, ,SROG
RTZOL DAG GIS DBU MAR 'BAB PA DANG, ,RIG PA'I BRTUL ZHUGS DAG
GIS RDO RJE NI, ,LTUNG MIN DE BZHIN STENG DU KHU BA STE, ,LAM
'DI DAG GIS SANGS RGYAS

@047B RNAMS KYI NI, ,BDE BA MCHOG TU 'GYUR BA MED PA ZHES,

SROG DBU MAR BCUG PAS RANG GI

SEMS KYI SNANG BA DU BA LA SOGS PAR SHAR BA'I MTSAN MA KHYAD PAR
CAN DAG DANG NI SROG RTZOL DAG GIS RTAG TU RLUNG DBU MAR 'BAB PA
DANG, 'DZIN PA SROG DANG THIG LE 'KHOR LO DRUG GI LTE BAR 'DOD
DGUR 'CHANG BA DANG, RJES DRAN

GYI SKABS KYI PHYAG CHEN RIG PA'I BRTUL ZHUGS DAG GIS RDO RJE
NOR BU'I PHYIR BYANG SEMS NI LTUNG BA MA YIN PA DANG, DE BZHIN
DU KHU BA DH'U T'I RU RANG GNAS BZUNG STE GTZUG TOR GYI BAR RIM
BZHIN STENG DU BRTZEGS TE MI 'GYUR BAR

BYED PA'I LAM 'DI CHOS CAN, KHYOD KYI RIM PA DAG GIS MCHOG GI
DNGOS GRUB MED NA MI 'BYUNG BA'I TSUL GYIS DNGOS SU BSKYED PA
YIN TE, KHYED KYIS SANGS RGYAS RNAMS KYIS NI BDE BA MCHOG TU
'GYUR BA MED PA ZHES RGYUD 'DI

PA'I MING GIS

'GRUB PAR 'GYUR BA YIN TE, KHYOD MCHOG DANG THUN MONG GI DNGOS
GRUB GANG

PHYAG RGYA CHEN MO GA LA ZHIG 'THOB STE MI 'THOB PA YIN PA'I

BDAG NYID DU 'DOD PA YIN TE, DUS NI KUN RDZOB STONG GZUGS KYI

SGRIB BRAL DU GYUR PA'I STONG NYID NI 'KHOR LO ZHES BRJOD PA
GANG ZHIG ,DE GNYIS DBYER MI PHYED PA YIN

PA'I PHYIR, DES NA DUS KYI 'KHOR LO 'DI YI DPAL NI MYUR DU THOB
PA'I SLAD DU RTAG TU PHYI NANG GI RNAL 'BYOR MA RNAMS KYI ZHABS
NI DRAN PAR BYED RIGS TE, RNAL 'BYOR PA GANG ZHIG PHYI NANG GI
RNAL 'BYOR MA RNAMS KYI ZHABS SGOM PA

DE'I PHYI NANG GI BGEGS NI RTAG TU NYAMS PAR 'GYUR PA YIN PA'I
PHYIR, GNYIS PA LA GNYIS, MDOR BSTAN PA DANG, RGYAS PAR BSHAD
PA'O, ,DANG PO STON PA LA, DGRA DANG SENG GE GLANG CHEN DBANG PO
MA DANG LTO 'GRO'I BDAG DANG

DANG BUD MED DANG BRAL MI BDAG 'KHRUGS PA'I 'JIGS DANG RDO RJE
LHUNG DANG NOR NYAMS RNAMS, ,

ZHIG GIS RDO RJE DBYANGS PHYUG MA SOGS PHYI'I RNAL 'BYOR MA

PHYI'I 'JIGS PA BCU DRUG DANG, THIG LE 'PHO BA'I 'GYUR BA'I
SGRIB PA

PA LA, RTZA 'KHOR RNAMS KYI LTE BA'I DBUS SU RLUNG DANG THIG LE
GA-YO MED DU 'DZIN PA'I 'DZIN PA SNGON DU 'GRO DGOS SHING, DE LA
RO RKYANG GI RGYU BA DBU MA 'BA' ZHIG NAS RGYU BA'I SROG RTZOL
SNGON DU 'GRO DGOS, DE LA THOG

MAR RLUNG DBU MAR BCUG NAS DBU MA SBYONG BAR BYED CING, STONG
GZUGS SNGAR MED GSAR DU BSGRUB PA SOR SDUD DANG, STONG GZUGS
GRUB PA BRTAN BYED BSAM GTAN GNYIS SNGON DU 'GRO DGOS PA'I
PHYIR, DE LTAR

NYAMS SU BLANGS PA'I 'BRAS BU LA CHUNG 'BRING CHEN PO GSUM LAS
DANG PO NI, ZHI RGYAS SOGS LAS RAB 'BYAMS DANG, GNYIS PA NI,
GRUB PA CHEN PO BRGYAD SOGS YIN LA, GSUM PA NI, SKU MTSAN DPES
BRGYAN PA

@182B STONG GZUGS YAB YUM ZHAL SBYOR GYI RNAM PA CAN DANG, THUGS
DAG PA GNYIS LDAN GYI CHOS NYID LA RTAG TU MNYAM PAR BZHAG PA'I
MCHOG TU MI 'GYUR BA'I BDE BA MTHAR THUG PA DE GNYIS NGO BO GCIG
PA'I RTEN DANG BRTEN

PAR GYUR PA SKAD CIG KYANG RGYUN MI 'CHAD PA'I GO 'PHANG DE NYID
YIN TE, RGYUD LAS, LUS NI DVANGS SHING RDUL PHRAN NYAMS PA NAM
MKHA' DANG MTSUNGS MTSAN LA SOGS PA RNAMS KYIS RAB RDZOGS GYUR,
,SNA TSOGS 'JIG RTEN

GSUM PO NYID NI DVANGS SHING SGRIB PA RNAM PAR BRAL BA RMI LAM
BZHIN DU SNANG, ,SKAD NI KUN NAS CHAD PA MED CING DU MA'I SKAD
GZHAN DAG GIS GZHAN GYI SNYING LA 'JUG PA STE, ,SEMS NI DAM PA'I
BDEBS GANG ZHING MI GA-YO

THAMS CAD DUS SU LHAN CIG SKYES PAS 'KHYUD PA'O, ZHES GSUNGS
PA'I PHYIR, SMRAS PA, KA L'A PA YI MDZES MA DRI MED 'OD, ,ZHING
'DI BTANG NAS RANG YUL PHYOGS PA'I TSE, ,RNAM DPYOD ZUR MIG
GA-YO BA'I GZHON

NU 'DI'I, ,MDZES SDUG LA CHAGS RE SHIG BGROD PA BSHOL, ,GANG GI
YON TAN BEEd'U RYA'I, ,RNA RGYAN ZUNG GIS RGYAL RNAMS KYANG,
,MTHO RIS DPA' MO BZHIN BRGYAN PA'I, ,BYED PO DANG PO'I SANGS
RGYAS RGYUD, ,GANG DE'I PHYI NANG

GZHAN GSUM GYI, ,ZAB DON 'O MA'I PAD MTSO CHER, ,MNGON PAR MDZES
PA'I 'DAB LDAN ZHIG ,LEGS BSHAD RDZA RNGA CI YANG RDUNG, ,GROGS
DAG MYUR DU SUM RTZEN DGA' BA'I TSAL, ,SA LA BABS 'DRA DPAL LDAN
SHAMBHA LA, ,

@183A *, ,KUN DGA'I 'BYOR PAS GANG BA'I ZHING KHAMS DER, ,'JUG
PAR 'DOD NA DAM PA'I LAM 'DIR ZHUGS, ,DE BZHIN NOR BU'I KHRI LA
SA BCU PA, ,MI DBANG GZUGS KYIS ROL PA'I ZHABS BSTEN CING, ,PHUN

TSOGS GSUNG GI BDUD RTZI 'THUNG 'DOD NA, ,LEGS BSHAD RGYA MTSO
CHE 'DIR 'JUG PA'I RIGS, ,KHYAD PAR DPAL LDAN DRAG PO 'KHOR LO
CAN, ,NAG PHYOGS 'JOMS SHING THUB BSTAN RDZOGS LDAN DU, ,'JOG
PA'I

NGO MTSAR DGA' STON MYONG 'DOD NA, ,LEGS BSHAD RGYA MTSO CHE
'DIR 'JUG PA'I RIGS, ,BDAG KYANG DENG NAS SKYE BA THAMS CAD DU,
,YID KYANG 'GYUR MED BDE DANG MI 'BRAL ZHING, ,RO 'DZIN LEGS
BSHAD GTAM 'DI'I

'BYOR PA DANG, ,SKAD CIG TZAM YANG 'BRAL BAR MA GYUR CIG ,ZAB
MO'I GNAS LA BYIS PA'I BLOS DPYAD PAS, ,NONGS PAR GYUR TSE LHA
DANG BLA MA LA, ,SNYING NAS 'CHAGS SO BRTZE BAS RJES BZUNG STE,
,NONGS PA RGYU BCAS

GZHOM PAR MDZAD DU GSOL, ,TSUL 'DIR 'BAD LAS BYUNG BA'I DGE BA
DES, ,SKYE DGU'I PHAN BDE RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA DANG, ,BDAG GI
BSHAD SGRUB LUNG RTOGS YON TAN RNAMS, ,LHAN CIG 'GRAN PA BZHIN
DU RGYAS

PAR SHOG ,CES BCOM LDAN 'DAS DPAL DUS KYI 'KHOR LO MCHOG GI DANG
PO'I SANGS RGYAS KYI RTZA BA'I RGYUD LAS PHYUNG BA BSDUS PA'I
RGYUD KYI RGYAS 'GREL DRI MA MED PA'I 'OD KYI RGYA CHER BSHAD PA
DE KHO NA NYID SNANG BA'I SNYING PO

@183B BSDUS PA YID BZHIN GYI NOR BU ZHES BYA BA 'DI NYID, SDE
SNOD GSUM DANG RGYUD SDE BZHI'I RNGA BO CHE RGYUN MAR SGROG
CING, BSLAB PA GSUM DANG RIM PA GNYIS KYI MNGON PAR RTOGS PAS
RGYUD PHYUG PA'I MDO SNGAGS RAB 'BYAMS

PA MANG PO LA ZIN THUN DU BYAS PA ZIN BRIS SU MDZAD PA RNAMS HA
CANG DAG PAR MI 'DUG PAS, DNGOS KYIS DAG POR BGYIS PA ZHIG DGOS
ZHES YANG YANG BSKUL BA DANG, BSTAN PA'I RTZA LAG CHOS KYI GDAN
KHRI 'DZIN PA'I

DAM PA DU MAS KYANG BSKUL BA LA BRTEN NAS, CHOS SMRA BA BLO
BZANG CHOS KYI RGYAL MTSAN GYIS CHOS GRVA CHEN PO BKRA SHIS LHUN
PO'I GZIMS KHANG DU SBYAR BA'I YI GE PA NI RAB 'BYAMS PA DAR MA
BZANG PO'O, ,'DIS KYANG

RGYAL BA'I BSTAN PA MI NUB PA'I RGYAL MTSAN DU GYUR CIG ,AE KA
PRiTZTSA,, ,,SARBA MANGGA LAm,, ` ,,AOm SVA STI DZ'A YA, DPAL
LDAN DANG PO'I SANGS RGYAS 'KHOR LO'I MGON, ,RGYUD RGYAL SDUD

MDZAD ZLA BA BZANG PO'I ZHABS, ,DBYER MED CHOS KYI RGYAL PO
TZONG KHA PA, ,BKA' DRIN MNYAM MED YAB SRAS RNAMS KYIS SKYONGS,
,BLO BZANG RGYAL BA'I CHOS KYI RGYAL SRID CHER, ,DBANG BSGYUR
BSHAD SGRUB BSTAN PA'I RGYAL

MTSAN 'DZIN, ,PHYOGS LAS RNAM PAR RGYAL BA'I DPAL MNGA' BA, ,RJE
BTZUN BLA MA LUS CAN GTZUG NA RGYAL, ,THABS SHES GNYIS MED DUS
KYI 'KHOR LO YI, ,RGYUD 'GREL DE NYID SNANG BA'I SNYING PO 'DIS,
,MTHA' DAG SKYE

@184A *, ,DGU'I RE BA SKONG BAS NA, ,LEGS BSHAD 'DI NI YID BZHIN
NOR BU'O, ,SA GSUM RIN CHEN GCIG GYUR NYIN BYED 'DIS, ,THUB
BSTAN GLING BZHI MDZES PAR BYA BA'I PHYIR, ,BLO BZANG RGYAL BA'I
BSTAN LA

RAB GUS SHING, ,KHYAD PAR RJE BTZUN BLA MAR MI PHYED PA'I, ,DAD
BRTZON 'PHRIN LAS SHING RTA'I KHA LO PA, ,JA SAG BLA MA 'PRIN
LAS CHOS 'PHEL GYIS, ,BKA' GDAMS SGRUB BRGYUD BSTAN PA'I 'BYUNG
GNAS MCHOG ,GRU 'DZIN

GNYIS PA GA-YAS RU GTZANG GI STOD, ,BKRA SHIS LHUN GYIS GRUB
PA'I CHOS GRVA CHER, ,RAB GSAL BAR GYI RTA LJANG BZHON PA LA,
,LEGS PAR 'GOD PA'I BRTZON PA DON YOD BYAS, ,'DIR 'BAD DGE BA
KUN TA LTAR DKAR DES, ,

BSTAN PA RIN CHEN PHYOGS BCUR RGYAS PA DANG, ,RJE BTZUN BLA MA'I
ZHABS PAD RAB BRTAN CING, ,'PHRIN LAS MNGA' THANG THUGS KYI
BZHED PA RNAMS, ,PHAN TSUN 'GRAN PA BZHIN DU 'PHEL BA DANG,
,KHYAD PAR RJE BTZUN CHOS KYI RGYAL

MTSAN GYIS, ,SKYE BA KUN TU 'BRAL MED RJES BZUNG NAS, ,BSLAB
GSUM LUNG RTOGS NOR BUS RGYUD GTAMS TE, ,BLA MED BYANG CHUB DAM
PA MYUR THOB SHOG ,BKOD LEGS YI GE'I BYED PO TSE BRTAN DANG,
,BRKOS KYI RIG BYED

DGE BSNYEN GROGS MCHED KYIS, ,LEGS PAR GZABS SHING 'DI YI DAG
